## üìÅ Project Structure

```sh
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ /
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ backend
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ __init__.py
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ __pycache__
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ auth.py
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ database.py
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ google_auth.py
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ main.py
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ migrations.py
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ models.py
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ rate_limiter.py
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ requirements.txt
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ schemas.py
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ services
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ static
    ‚îÇ   ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ tasks.py
    ‚îÇ   ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ templates
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ brand_generator.db
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ requirements.txt
    ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ run.py
    ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ venv
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Include
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Lib
        ‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ pyvenv.cfg
        ‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Scripts
```

## üöÄ Getting Started

### üìã Prerequisites

This project requires the following dependencies:

- **Programming Language:** Python
- **Package Manager:** Pip, Cargo

### ‚öôÔ∏è Installation

Build  from the source and intsall dependencies:

1. **Clone the repository:**

    ```sh
    ‚ùØ git clone ../
    ```

2. **Navigate to the project directory:**

    ```sh
    ‚ùØ cd 
    ```

3. **Install the dependencies:**

<!-- SHIELDS BADGE CURRENTLY DISABLED -->
	<!-- [![pip][pip-shield]][pip-link] -->
	<!-- REFERENCE LINKS -->
	<!-- [pip-shield]: https://img.shields.io/badge/Pip-3776AB.svg?style={badge_style}&logo=pypi&logoColor=white -->
	<!-- [pip-link]: https://pypi.org/project/pip/ -->

	**Using [pip](https://pypi.org/project/pip/):**

	```sh
	‚ùØ pip install -r requirements.txt, backend\requirements.txt
	```
<!-- SHIELDS BADGE CURRENTLY DISABLED -->
	<!-- [![cargo][cargo-shield]][cargo-link] -->
	<!-- REFERENCE LINKS -->
	<!-- [cargo-shield]: None -->
	<!-- [cargo-link]: None -->

	**Using [cargo](None):**

	```sh
	‚ùØ echo 'INSERT-INSTALL-COMMAND-HERE'
	```

### üíª Usage

Run the project with:

**Using [pip](https://pypi.org/project/pip/):**
```sh
python {entrypoint}
```
**Using [cargo](None):**
```sh
echo 'INSERT-RUN-COMMAND-HERE'
```

### üß™ Testing

 uses the {__test_framework__} test framework. Run the test suite with:

**Using [pip](https://pypi.org/project/pip/):**
```sh
pytest
```
**Using [cargo](None):**
```sh
echo 'INSERT-TEST-COMMAND-HERE'
```

## ü§ù Contributing

- **üí¨ [Join the Discussions](https://LOCAL///discussions)**: Share your insights, provide feedback, or ask questions.
- **üêõ [Report Issues](https://LOCAL///issues)**: Submit bugs found or log feature requests for the `` project.
- **üí° [Submit Pull Requests](https://LOCAL///blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md)**: Review open PRs, and submit your own PRs.

<details closed>
<summary>Contributing Guidelines</summary>

1. **Fork the Repository**: Start by forking the project repository to your LOCAL account.
2. **Clone Locally**: Clone the forked repository to your local machine using a git client.
   ```sh
   git clone .
   ```
3. **Create a New Branch**: Always work on a new branch, giving it a descriptive name.
   ```sh
   git checkout -b new-feature-x
   ```
4. **Make Your Changes**: Develop and test your changes locally.
5. **Commit Your Changes**: Commit with a clear message describing your updates.
   ```sh
   git commit -m 'Implemented new feature x.'
   ```
6. **Push to LOCAL**: Push the changes to your forked repository.
   ```sh
   git push origin new-feature-x
   ```
7. **Submit a Pull Request**: Create a PR against the original project repository. Clearly describe the changes and their motivations.
8. **Review**: Once your PR is reviewed and approved, it will be merged into the main branch. Congratulations on your contribution!
</details>
